msg:I have to praise this hotel here. I didn't expect much when I booked it, but I didn't expect it to give me a big surprise.
First of all, the room is clean and dry, parking is timely, and the service attitude is friendly.
Let me talk about a few amazing details: First of all, the sea view of the sea view suite we booked is really invincible. The Boao sea view at 3 pm is absolutely beautiful.
The second point is that the hotel's smart toilet is very smart. It is not an ordinary smart toilet cover. It has very complete functions. Many five-star hotels are not equipped with such advanced smart toilets, which makes people feel happy.
The third point is that although the hotel's swimming pool is not big, it is clean, comfortable and well maintained, which is very suitable for children to swim.
The fourth point is that although the hotel's children's playground is indoors and the area is not large, it is very playable. There are no fancy money-eating machines, just climbing cars, trampolines, etc., and the children have a lot of fun.
The fifth point is that it is very close to the beach, the waves are very gentle and the sand is fine, which is suitable for children to play.
A suggestion is that the breakfast preparation is not sufficient. In the case of a surge in tourists, I feel that the restaurant is not responsive enough and the dishes are added slowly.
Finally, let's talk about the travel photography. It is very beautiful, mainly because of the blessing of the beautiful scenery. The experience is really great. I will book it next time.

msg:I have been procrastinating for a long time and I have not had time to write this review.
The trip was planned for a long time. Boao gave me a great overall feeling. This hotel impressed me especially.
The overall decoration style is very island resort style, and there is a ceiling fan in the room. It is retro. The full sea view room upgraded to us has a particularly wide view, and the sea breeze blows, leisurely and happy~
The location is about 2 kilometers away from Boao Town. Because I brought Xiaobao with me, I took a Didi taxi. In fact, there are many ** electric vehicles nearby, and many tourists rent them. I think couples can ride to the town to solve the dining problem.
The service staff are very friendly as a whole. From the boys and girls at the front desk, to an old man in the lobby, and the tall and thin supervisor of the restaurant, everyone is working very hard. Every time I meet these people, I will take the initiative to say hello. As long as there is water stains near the coffee machine in the dining area, someone will deal with it in time. The floor of the lobby is always cleaned because tourists who often swim on the beach pass by. These details made me decide that I will come here again next time.
If I have to say the shortcomings, I hope this hotel can be loved and recognized by more people. I think there are two points: the cleaning of the sofa in the room was neglected and there was a peculiar smell. It is recommended to check and replace it. The facilities of the children's playground on the first floor are great, but it is very hot without air conditioning, and one of the only three fans is still broken. It is recommended to deal with it and replace it. I wish Daoji Seaview will get better and better.

msg:Divide it into two parts
Deduction items:
1. Like some previous reviews, the room cleaning was found to have not been done during check-in, and there were unfinished coke left by the last guest. This hope the hotel must pay attention to it.
2. Facilities need to be upgraded. It‚Äôs a big room with few plugs, and you have to unplug the lamp to free up the plug for charging. This doesn‚Äôt feel good
3. Too many cabinets are actually useless. The common safes in four-star and five-star hotels do not. After all, there must be some valuables (such as the camera and drone I brought), and I can't bring it with me at any time. I hope to make up for it.
3. This lobby is really not like a four-star hotel lobby. It is not open and a**ospheric. Although it does not affect the accommodation, it will definitely have some impact on new guests.
bonus
1. The location is very good, very close to the beach. The beach is not close, long and wide, and very flat. It is very safe to get to the belly button when it is far away from the sea. Swimming is average, but playing with waves is great. The waves here are relatively large, but not dangerous. It is especially suitable for guests who don‚Äôt know how to swim and want to feel in the sea. Observed these few days, there are not many people, but there are shower facilities on the beach, which is really awesome. Not to mention the softness of the sand, the key is that there are no shells that are common on other beaches, and it is perfect to walk up without piercing your feet.
2. The service is still good. The front desk, cleaners and restaurant staff are polite and respect the guests. This is still in line with the four-star standard.
3. Although the hotel is about three kilometers away from Boao Town (a lively place), it is particularly good for taxis. Generally, the order is received within ten seconds, and it is less than ten yuan to go to the town. There is also a small yellow car at Xiaojiekou downstairs, so you can ride it yourself, which is convenient. We can walk back to the hotel from Boao Town along the beach or Binhai Road, and it takes only half an hour. The road is good (only a short distance from the hotel is not so good, but you can borrow the beach park).
4. The restaurant is not expensive (of course it is relative), and it is acceptable to travel out. The breakfast is full of varieties (Chinese, Western, and local). Basically, there are seats when you come.
5. After living for a few days, I feel that the air conditioner works well. However, the toiletries are average, and there is still a gap between the four stars. A deposit is required for check-in (Alipay WeChat can be used), and it will be credited soon after check-out.
If the interior design of this hotel is upgraded to be more modern, I think it is difficult to compare with other hotels in the vicinity.

A beautiful small town, with woods next to the hotel, and on the main road outside, we often see little squirrels running around, as well as hoopoe, a second-level national protected animal. The ecology is really good.
